S\u1ef1 tho\u00e1i lui tr\u01b0\u1edbc halving (Pre-Halving retrace)\n\nM\u1ed9t giai \u0111o\u1ea1n tho\u00e1i lui tr\u01b0\u1edbc halving th\u01b0\u1eddng di\u1ec5n ra xung quanh s\u1ef1 ki\u1ec7n halving ch\u00ednh (v\u00f2ng m\u00e0u xanh \u0111\u1eadm)\n\nN\u0103m 2016, giai \u0111o\u1ea1n n\u00e0y \u0111\u00e3 gi\u1ea3m s\u00e2u -38%\n\nN\u0103m 2020, giai \u0111o\u1ea1n n\u00e0y gi\u1ea3m s\u00e2u -20%\n\nS\u1ef1 tho\u00e1i lui tr\u01b0\u1edbc halving n\u00e0y khi\u1ebfn nh\u00e0 \u0111\u1ea7u t\u01b0 \u0111\u1eb7t c\u00e2u h\u1ecfi li\u1ec7u halving c\u00f3 th\u1ef1c s\u1ef1 l\u00e0 y\u1ebfu t\u1ed1 t\u0103ng gi\u00e1 hay kh\u00f4ng?\n\n4. Giai \u0111o\u1ea1n T\u00e1i t\u00edch lu\u1ef9 (Re-Accumulation)\n\nGiai \u0111o\u1ea1n tho\u00e1i lui tr\u01b0\u1edbc halving \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c theo sau b\u1edfi giai \u0111o\u1ea1n t\u00e1i t\u00edch lu\u1ef9 k\u00e9o d\u00e0i trong nhi\u1ec1u th\u00e1ng (m\u00e0u \u0111\u1ecf)\n\nNhi\u1ec1u nh\u00e0 \u0111\u1ea7u t\u01b0 b\u1ecb lo\u1ea1i b\u1ecf trong giai \u0111o\u1ea1n n\u00e0y do s\u1ef1 bu\u1ed3n ch\u00e1n, kh\u00f4ng ki\u00ean nh\u1eabn v\u00e0 th\u1ea5t v\u1ecdng v\u00ec kh\u00f4ng \u0111\u1ea1t \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c k\u1ebft qu\u1ea3 mong mu\u1ed1n trong \u0111\u1ea7u t\u01b0 BTC c\u1ee7a h\u1ecd ngay sau halving\n\n5. Xu h\u01b0\u1edbng t\u0103ng c\u1ea5p t\u1ed1c (Parabolic Uptrend)\n\nKhi Bitcoin b\u1ee9t ph\u00e1 ra kh\u1ecfi khu v\u1ef1c t\u00e1i t\u00edch lu\u1ef9 v\u00e0 v\u00e0o xu h\u01b0\u1edbng t\u0103ng c\u1ea5p t\u1ed1c (m\u00e0u xanh)\n\nTrong giai \u0111o\u1ea1n n\u00e0y, Bitcoin tr\u1ea3i qua s\u1ef1 t\u0103ng tr\u01b0\u1edfng nhanh ch\u00f3ng tr\u00ean \u0111\u01b0\u1eddng \u0111\u1ebfn c\u00e1c m\u1ee9c gi\u00e1 k\u1ef7 l\u1ee5c m\u1edbi\n\n#Crypto  #Bitcoin", "replyCount": 8, "retweetCount": 0, "likeCount": 11, "quoteCount": 0, "conversationId": 1710540661081198662, "hashtags": ["BTC"], "cashtags": [], "mentionedUsers": [], "links": [], "viewCount": 268, "retweetedTweet": null, "quotedTweet": null, "place": null, "coordinates": null, "inReplyToTweetId": null, "inReplyToUser": null, "source": "<a href=\"http://twitter.com/download/android\" rel=\"nofollow\">Twitter for Android</a>", "sourceUrl": "http://twitter.com/download/android", "sourceLabel": "Twitter for Android", "media": {"photos": [{"url": "https://pbs.twimg.com/media/F70PqlrbMAAgx9i.jpg"}], "videos": [], "animated": []}, "_type": "snscrape.modules.twitter.Tweet"}
